 \n  private updateState(partial: Partial<BrainState>): void {\n    this.state = { ...this.state, ...partial };\n    this.listeners.forEach(l => l(this.state));\n  }\n  \n  getState(): BrainState {\n    return { ...this.state };\n  }\n  \n  subscribe(listener: (s: BrainState) => void): () => void {\n    this.listeners.add(listener);\n    listener(this.state);\n    return () =>  \n  start(): void {\n    if (!this.init()) return;\n    \n    // Cannot start while speaking (Audio Mutex)\n    if (this.state.audioState === 'SPEAKING') {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Cannot  \n  speak(text: string, emotion: string = 'neutral', onDone?: () => void): void {\n    if (!text || this.state.mode === 'text') {\n      onDone?.();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    if (!this.init() 2;\n  const targetY = rect.top + rect.height / 2;\n  \n  const p = createPointer();\n  \n  // Start from current position or center\n  const startX = parseFloat(p.style.left) || window.innerWidth / 2;\n  const startY = parseFloat(p.style.top) || window.innerHeight / 2;\n  \n  p.style.display = 'block';\n  p.style.left = `${startX}px`;\n  p.style.top = `${startY}px`;\n  \n  // Create trail effect\n  const steps = 10;\n  for (let i = 1; i <= steps; i++) {\n    setTimeout(() => {\n      const progress = i / steps;\n      const x = startX + (targetX - startX) * progress;\n      const y = startY + (targetY - startY) * progress;\n      createTrail(x, y);\n    }, i * 50);\n  }\n  \n  // Animate to target\n  await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 50));\n  p.style.left = `${targetX}px`;\n  p.style.top = `${targetY}px`;\n  \n  // Wait for animation\n  await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 600));\n}\n\nasync function clickElement(element: HTMLElement): Promise<void> {\n  // Add highlight\n    }\n  }\n  \n  return null;\n}\n\nfunction findElement(target: string): HTMLElement | null {\n  // Find matching target definition\n  const targetDef = CLICK_TARGETS.find(t => \n    t.keywords.some(k => target.includes(k) || k.includes(target))\n  );\n  \n  if (targetDef) {\n    // Try each selector\n    for (const selector of targetDef.selectors) {\n      try {\n        // Handle :contains pseudo-selector\n        if (selector.includes(':contains(')) {\n          const match = selector.match(/(.+):contains\\(\"(.+)\"\\)/);\n          if (match) {\n            const [, baseSelector, text] = match;\n            const elements = document.querySelectorAll(baseSelector || '*');\n            for (const el of elements) {\n              if (el.textContent?.includes(text)) {\n                return el as HTMLElement;\n              }\n            }\n          }\n        } else {\n          const el = document.querySelector(selector);\n          if (el) return el as HTMLElement;\n        }\n      } catch (e) {\n        // Invalid selector, continue\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Try by text content\n    return findElementByText(targetDef.label);\n  }\n  \n  // '/',\n      'about': '/about',\n      'howitworks': '/how-it-works',\n      'partners': '/partners',\n      'lend': '/lend',\n      'realestate': '/real-estate',\n      'products': '/products'\n    };\n    \n    const route = routes[target];\n    if (route && window.location.pathname !== route) {\n      window.location.href = route;\n      return true;\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  \n  if VendorPhone: React.FC<Props> = ({ value, onChange, onNext }) => {\n  const [digits, setDigits] = useState(value.replace(/\\D/g, ''));\n  \n  const handleDigits = useCallback((d: string) => {\n    setDigits(prev => {\n      const next = (prev + d).slice(0, 10);\n      onChange(next);\n      if (next.length === 10) {\n        speak(`Got it! ${formatPhone(next)}. Welcome aboard, partner.', 'excited', () => onVerified());\n    } else {\n      setError('Invalid code. Demo code is 123456');\n      speak('That code is invalid. For this demo, say one two three four five six.', 'concerned');\n    }\n  }, [onVerified]);\n  \n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\n    setOtp(prev => {\n      const filled = prev.filter(d => d).length;\n      const next = [...prev];\n      let idx = filled;\n      \n      for (const d of digits) {\n        if (idx < 6) {\n          next[idx] = d;\n          idx++;\n        }\n      }\n      \n      if (next.filter(d => d).length === 6) {\n        setTimeout(() => verifyCode(next.join('')), 300);\n      }\n      \n      return next;\n    });\n  }, [verifyCode]);\n  \n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\n    if (cmd.includes('clear') || cmd.includes('reset') || cmd.includes('start over')) {\n      setOtp(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\n      setError('');\n      speak('Cleared. Go ahead with the code.', 'neutral');\n    }\n  }, []);\n  \n  useEffect(() => {\n    const u1 = onDigits(handleDigits);\n    const u2 = onCommand(handleCommand);\n    return () => { u1(); u2(); };\n  }, [handleDigits, handleCommand]);\n  \n  const handleInput = (index: number, value: string) => {\n    if (!/^\\d*$/.test(value)) return;\n    const next = [...otp];\n    next[index] = value.slice(-1);\n    setOtp(next);\n    if (value && index < 5) inputRefs.current[index + 1]?.focus();\n    if (next.every(d => d)) verifyCode(next.join(''));\n  };\n  \n  return (\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\ud83d\udd10</span>\n      <h3 style={{ color: '#B8860B', margin: '16px 0 8px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\n        Verification Code\n      </h3>\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\n        Code sent to {phone}\n      </p>\n      \n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '12px', marginBottom: '20px' }}>\n        {otp.map((digit, idx) => (\n          <input\n            key={idx}\n            ref={el => inputRefs.current[idx] = el}\n            type=\"text\"\n            inputMode=\"numeric\"\n            maxLength={1}\n            value={digit}\n            onChange={e => handleInput(idx, e.target.value)}\n            style={{\n              width: '55px',\n              height: '68px',\n              fontSize: '2em',\n              textAlign: 'center',\n              borderRadius: '12px',\n              border: `3px solid ${digit ? '#4CAF50' : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.4)'}`,\n              background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n              color: '#fff'\n            }}\n          />\n        ))}\n      </div>\n      \n      {error && <p style={{ color: '#f44336', marginBottom: '16px' }}>{error}</p>}\n      <p style={{ color: '#555', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\ud83d\udca1 Demo code: 123456</p>\n      \n      <AgenticBar\n        context=\"OTP Verification\"\n        hints={['\"one two three four five six\"', '\"clear\" to reset']}\n        welcomeMessage=\"Enter the 6-digit verification code. count, defaulting to 5');\n    pages = 5;\n  }\n  \n  // Detect category from filename\n  const lower = originalName.toLowerCase();\n  let category = 'home';\n  if (lower.includes('furniture') || category = 'outdoor';\n  else if (lower.includes('light') || lower.includes('lamp')) category = 'lighting';\n  else if (lower.includes('bath') || lower.includes('sanitary')) category = 'bathroom';\n type AudioState = 'IDLE' | 'LISTENING' | 'THINKING' | 'SPEAKING' | 'PAUSED';\\nexport type VoiceMode = 'interactive' | 'talkative' | 'text';\\n\\ninterface BrainState {\\n  audioState: AudioState;\\n  mode: VoiceMode;\\n  transcript: string;\\n  interim: string;\\n  context: string;\\n  error: string | null;\\n  lastCommand: string;\\n  isProcessing: boolean;\\n}\\n\\n// Word to digit mapping\\nconst W2D: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0', 'one': '1', 'won': '1',\\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2', 'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8', 'nine': '9', 'nein': '9', 'ten': '10'\\n};\\n\\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\\\s+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  for (const w of words) {\\n    if (W2D[w]) digits += W2D[w];\\n    else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(w)) digits += w;\\n  }\\n  return digits || text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n};\\n\\nexport const formatPhone = (d: string): string => {\\n  const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3, 6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\nclass VoiceBrain {\\n  private static instance: VoiceBrain;\\n  \\n  // Core '',\\n    isProcessing: false\\n  };\\n  \\n  // Handlers\\n  private listeners = new Set<(s: BrainState) => void>();\\n  private digitHandlers = new Set<(d: string) => void>();\\n  private       setTimeout(() => voiceBrain.start(), 500);\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }, [welcomeMessage, autoStart]);\\n  \\n  // Handle text input submit\\n  const handleTextSubmit = useCallback(() => {\\n    if from 'react';\\nimport AgenticBar, { speak, onDigits, onCommand, formatPhone } from '../../../agentic';\\n\\ninterface Props {\\n  value: string;\\n  onChange: (phone: string) => void;\\n  onNext: () => void;\\n}\\n\\nconst VendorPhone: React.FC<Props> = ({ value, onChange, onNext }) => {\\n  const [digits, setDigits] = useState(value.replace(/\\\\D/g, ''));\\n  \\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((d: string) => {\\n    setDigits(prev => {\\n      const next = (prev + d).slice(0, 10);\\n      onChange(next);\\n      if (next.length === 10) {\\n        speak(`Got it! ${formatPhone(next)}. Say yes to confirm, or clear to start over.`, 'happy');\\n      } else if (d) {\\n        speak(`${10 - next.length} more digits.`, 'neutral');\\n      }\\n      return next;\\n    });\\n  }, [onChange]);\\n  \\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    if ((cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('confirm') || cmd.includes('correct') || cmd.includes('send')) && digits.length >= 10) {\\n      speak('Sending verification code now.', 'happy', () => onNext());\\n    }\\n    if (cmd.includes('clear') || cmd.includes('reset') || cmd.includes('start over')) {\\n      setDigits('');\\n      onChange('');\\n      speak('Cleared. Go ahead and tell me your number again.', 'neutral');\\n    }\\n    if (cmd.includes('no') || cmd.includes('wrong')) {\\n      setDigits('');\\n      onChange('');\\n      speak('No problem, cleared. Tell me the correct number.', 'neutral');\\n    }\\n  }, [digits, onChange, onNext]);\\n  \\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const u1 = onDigits(handleDigits);\\n    const u2 = onCommand(handleCommand);\\n    return () => { u1(); u2(); };\\n  }, [handleDigits, handleCommand]);\\n  \\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const clean = value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    if (clean !== digits) setDigits(clean);\\n  }, [value]);\\n  \\n  const canSubmit = digits.length >= 10;\\n  \\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\ud83d\\udcf1</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: '#B8860B', margin: '16px 0 8px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\\n        Enter Your Phone Number\\n      </h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        Say digits like \\\"seven zero three\\\" or type below\\n      </p>\\n      \\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '12px', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '1.5em' }}>+1</span>\\n        <input\\n          type=\\\"tel\\\"\\n          value={formatPhone(digits)}\\n          onChange={e => {\\n            const clean = e.target.value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n            setDigits(clean);\\n            onChange(clean);\\n          }}\\n          placeholder=\\\"000-000-0000\\\"\\n          style={{\\n            fontSize: '2em',\\n            padding: '18px 28px',\\n            borderRadius: '14px',\\n            border: `3px solid ${canSubmit ? Welcome aboard, partner.', 'excited', () => onVerified());\\n    } else {\\n      setError('Invalid code. Demo code is 123456');\\n      speak('That code is invalid. For this demo, say one two three four five six.', 'concerned');\\n    }\\n  }, [onVerified]);\\n  \\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    setOtp(prev => {\\n      const filled = prev.filter(d => d).length;\\n      const next = [...prev];\\n      let idx = filled;\\n      \\n      for (const d of digits) {\\n        if (idx < 6) {\\n          next[idx] = d;\\n          idx++;\\n        }\\n      }\\n      \\n      if (next.filter(d => d).length === 6) {\\n        setTimeout(() => verifyCode(next.join('')), 300);\\n      }\\n      \\n      return next;\\n    });\\n  }, [verifyCode]);\\n  \\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    if (cmd.includes('clear') || cmd.includes('reset') || cmd.includes('start over')) {\\n      setOtp(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\\n      setError('');\\n      speak('Cleared. Go ahead with the code.', 'neutral');\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const u1 = onDigits(handleDigits);\\n    const u2 = onCommand(handleCommand);\\n    return () => { u1(); u2(); };\\n  }, [handleDigits, handleCommand]);\\n  \\n  const handleInput = (index: number, value: string) => {\\n    if (!/^\\\\d*$/.test(value)) return;\\n    const next = [...otp];\\n    next[index] = value.slice(-1);\\n    setOtp(next);\\n    if (value && index < 5) inputRefs.current[index + 1]?.focus();\\n    if (next.every(d => d)) verifyCode(next.join(''));\\n  };\\n  \\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\ud83d\\udd10</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: '#B8860B', margin: '16px 0 8px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\\n        Verification Code\\n      </h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        Code sent to {phone}\\n      </p>\\n      \\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '12px', marginBottom: '20px' }}>\\n        {otp.map((digit, idx) => (\\n          <input\\n            key={idx}\\n            ref={el => inputRefs.current[idx] = el}\\n            type=\\\"text\\\"\\n            inputMode=\\\"numeric\\\"\\n            maxLength={1}\\n            value={digit}\\n            onChange={e => handleInput(idx, e.target.value)}\\n            style={{\\n              width: '55px',\\n              height: '68px',\\n              fontSize: '2em',\\n              textAlign: 'center',\\n              borderRadius: '12px',\\n              border: `3px solid ${digit ? '#4CAF50' : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.4)'}`,\\n              background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n              color: '#fff'\\n            }}\\n          />\\n        ))}\\n      </div>\\n      \\n      {error && <p style={{ color: '#f44336', marginBottom: '16px' }}>{error}</p>}\\n      <p style={{ color: '#555', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\\ud83d\\udca1 Demo code: 123456</p>\\n      \\n      <AgenticBar\\n        context=\\\"OTP Verification\\\"\\n        hints={['\\\"one two three four five six\\\"', '\\\"clear\\\" to reset']}\\n        welcomeMessage=\\\"Enter the 6-digit verification code. For this demo, say one two three four five six.\\\"\\n        showTypeInput={false}\\n      />\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n};\\n\\nexport default VendorOTP;\\nVOEOF\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 VendorOTP.tsx updated\\\"\\n\\n# VendorProfile\\necho \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"[UPDATE] VendorProfile.tsx...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VDIR/VendorProfile.tsx\\\" << 'VPREOF'\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';\\nimport AgenticBar, { speak, onCommand } from '../../../agentic';\\n\\ninterface Props {\\n  profile: string;\\n  beautified: string;\\n  companyName: string;\\n  onChange: (profile: string) => void;\\n  onCompanyChange: (name: string) => void;\\n  onBeautify: (beautified: string) => void;\\n  onSave: () => void;\\n}\\n\\nconst VendorProfile: React.FC<Props> = ({\\n  profile,\\n  beautified,\\n  companyName,\\n  onChange,\\n  onCompanyChange,\\n  onBeautify,\\n  onSave\\n}) => {\\n  const [isBeautifying, setIsBeautifying] = useState(false);\\n  const [showBeautified, setShowBeautified] = useState(!!beautified);\\n  \\n  const doBeautify = useCallback(() => {\\n    if (!profile.trim() && !companyName.trim()) {\\n      speak('Please enter your company name and description first.', 'concerned');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    setIsBeautifying(true);\\n    speak('Enhancing your profile with AI magic...', 'thinking');\\n    \\n    setTimeout(() => {\\n      const enhanced = `\\ud83c\\udfe2 ${companyName || 'Your Company'}\\n\\nPremium solutions provider specializing in ${profile || 'quality products and services'}.\\n\\n\\u2728 Why Choose Us:\\n\\u2022 Exceptional quality and craftsmanship\\n\\u2022 Customer-focused service excellence\\n\\u2022 Competitive pricing with premium value\\n\\u2022 Fast and reliable delivery\\n\\n\\ud83c\\udf1f Trusted by homeowners and designers on VistaView -
